{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_015bxLzV9mxHuJEXY9KWmPyW","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# Specification: `superclaude roadmap` CLI Command\n     2→\n     3→**Version**: v1.1\n     4→**Status**: Draft\n     5→**Date**: 2026-03-04\n     6→**Source**: Brainstorming session + sc:spec-panel review\n     7→**Output directory**: `.dev/releases/current/v2.06-RoadmapCLI/`\n     8→\n     9→---\n    10→\n    11→## 1. Problem Statement\n    12→\n    13→The `/sc:roadmap` skill executes inside a single Claude Code context where all steps — extraction, variant generation, adversarial debate, merge — run as behavioral instructions within the same session. This makes fabrication structurally possible: Claude can skip expensive steps (e.g. actually invoking sc:adversarial-protocol) and self-report completion. The skill-to-skill invocation chain fails silently.\n    14→\n    15→**Root cause**: Claude controls its own workflow. Nothing external enforces step completion before the next step begins.\n    16→\n    17→**Solution**: A CLI command (`superclaude roadmap`) that acts as a conductor — calling Claude as a subprocess once per step, with a file-on-disk gate between each step. Claude cannot advance to step N+1 because the CLI hasn't issued that prompt yet. Fabrication becomes impossible without writing the required output files.\n    18→\n    19→<!-- Source: Variant B (tasklist-strategies), Strategy 1 rationale — merged per Change #3 -->\n    20→\n    21→**Design principle — no circular self-validation**: The conductor enforces a strict trust boundary. Gate validation (`gate_passed()`) is pure Python — it never invokes Claude to evaluate Claude's output. This eliminates the circular self-validation failure mode where the same model that produced an artifact judges its own quality, which produces false confidence regardless of how sophisticated the validation criteria are. The insight that \"the same model that produces output cannot reliably validate its own intermediate state\" (from adversarial analysis of tasklist pipeline strategies) is the architectural justification for externalizing all gate logic into deterministic Python.\n    22→\n    23→---\n    24→\n    25→## 2. Scope\n    26→\n    27→### In Scope (v1)\n    28→- `superclaude roadmap <spec-file>` CLI command\n    29→- 8-step pipeline (extract → generate-A/B in parallel → diff → debate → score → merge → test-strategy)\n    30→- Shared `pipeline/` base module extracted from `sprint/`\n    31→- Sprint migration to use `pipeline/` internals\n    32→- Gate validation: file existence + YAML frontmatter fields + minimum line count\n    33→- Retry-once-then-halt failure policy\n    34→- `--resume` flag for restarting from failed step\n    35→- `--dry-run` flag for plan preview\n    36→- Single PR delivery (pipeline/ extraction + sprint migration + roadmap/ all together)\n    37→\n    38→### Out of Scope (v1)\n    39→- TUI / rich progress display (stdout logging only)\n    40→- `--blind` adversarial mode flag\n    41→- Multi-spec consolidation (`--specs`)\n    42→- Tasklist generation from roadmap output\n    43→- `--agents` count > 2 (v1 supports exactly 2 agents for generate-A / generate-B)\n    44→\n    45→### 2.1 Design Constraints\n    46→<!-- Source: Variant B (tasklist-strategies), scope discipline — merged per Change #4 -->\n    47→\n    48→- **YAGNI enforcement**: The `pipeline/` module implements only patterns required by `sprint/` and `roadmap/`. No speculative abstractions for hypothetical future commands.\n    49→- **Conductor minimalism**: The conductor's responsibility is step sequencing, gate enforcement, retry logic, and state management. It does not interpret, evaluate, or transform artifact content.\n    50→- **No self-validation**: Gate checks are pure Python. The conductor never invokes Claude to judge Claude's output (see §1 design principle).\n    51→- **Deferral tracking**: Features considered and deferred are recorded in §11 with rationale, preserving decision provenance for future versions.\n    52→\n    53→---\n    54→\n    55→## 3. Problem Statement\n\nThe `/sc:roadmap` skill executes inside a single Claude Code context where all steps — extraction, variant generation, adversarial debate, merge — run as behavioral instructions within the same session. This makes fabrication structurally possible: Claude can skip expensive steps (e.g. actually invoking sc:adversarial-protocol) and self-report completion. The skill-to-skill invocation chain fails silently.\n\n**Root cause**: Claude controls its own workflow. Nothing external enforces step completion before the next step begins.\n\n**Solution**: A CLI command (`superclaude roadmap`) that acts as a conductor — calling Claude as a subprocess once per step, with a file-on-disk gate between each step. Claude cannot advance to step N+1 because the CLI hasn't issued that prompt yet. Fabrication becomes impossible without writing the required output files.\n\n<!-- Source: Variant B (tasklist-strategies), Strategy 1 rationale — merged per Change #3 -->\n\n**Design principle — no circular self-validation**: The conductor enforces a strict trust boundary. Gate validation (`gate_passed()`) is pure Python — it never invokes Claude to evaluate Claude's output. This eliminates the circular self-validation failure mode where the same model that produced an artifact judges its own quality, which produces false confidence regardless of how sophisticated the validation criteria are. The insight that \"the same model that produces output cannot reliably validate its own intermediate state\" (from adversarial analysis of tasklist pipeline strategies) is the architectural justification for externalizing all gate logic into deterministic Python.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Scope\n\n### In Scope (v1)\n- `superclaude roadmap <spec-file>` CLI command\n- 8-step pipeline (extract → generate-A/B in parallel → diff → debate → score → merge → test-strategy)\n- Shared `pipeline/` base module extracted from `sprint/`\n- Sprint migration to use `pipeline/` internals\n- Gate validation: file existence + YAML frontmatter fields + minimum line count\n- Retry-once-then-halt failure policy\n- `--resume` flag for restarting from failed step\n- `--dry-run` flag for plan preview\n- Single PR delivery (pipeline/ extraction + sprint migration + roadmap/ all together)\n\n### Out of Scope (v1)\n- TUI / rich progress display (stdout logging only)\n- `--blind` adversarial mode flag\n- Multi-spec consolidation (`--specs`)\n- Tasklist generation from roadmap output\n- `--agents` count > 2 (v1 supports exactly 2 agents for generate-A / generate-B)\n\n### 2.1 Design Constraints\n<!-- Source: Variant B (tasklist-strategies), scope discipline — merged per Change #4 -->\n\n- **YAGNI enforcement**: The `pipeline/` module implements only patterns required by `sprint/` and `roadmap/`. No speculative abstractions for hypothetical future commands.\n- **Conductor minimalism**: The conductor's responsibility is step sequencing, gate enforcement, retry logic, and state management. It does not interpret, evaluate, or transform artifact content.\n- **No self-validation**: Gate checks are pure Python. The conductor never invokes Claude to judge Claude's output (see §1 design principle).\n- **Deferral tracking**: Features considered and deferred are recorded in §11 with rationale, preserving decision provenance for future versions.\n\n---\n\n## 3. By default this is the parent directory of `spec_file`:\n   275→\n   276→```\n   277→spec:   .dev/releases/current/v2.07/spec.md\n   278→output: .dev/releases/current/v2.07/\n   279→  extraction.md\n   280→  roadmap-opus-architect.md\n   281→  roadmap-haiku-architect.md\n   282→  diff-analysis.md\n   283→  debate-transcript.md\n   284→  base-selection.md\n   285→  roadmap.md\n   286→  test-strategy.md\n   287→```\n   288→\n   289→---\n   290→\n   291→## 5. CLI Interface\n   292→\n   293→```\n   294→superclaude roadmap <spec-file> [OPTIONS]\n   295→\n   296→Arguments:\n   297→  spec-file          Path to specification markdown file (required)\n   298→\n   299→Options:\n   300→  --agents TEXT      Comma-separated agent specs: model[:persona]\n   301→                     Default: \"opus:architect,haiku:architect\"\n   302→                     Model shorthand (opus/sonnet/haiku) passed directly to\n   303→                     claude CLI — no resolution required.\n   304→\n   305→  --output PATH      Output directory for all artifacts.\n   306→                     Default: parent directory of spec-file.\n   307→\n   308→  --depth [quick|standard|deep]\n   309→                     Controls debate step round count.\n   310→                     quick=1 round, standard=2, deep=3.\n   311→                     Default: standard\n   312→\n   313→  --resume           Skip steps whose output files already pass their gates.\n   314→                     Re-run from the first step that fails its gate.\n   315→                     If spec-file has changed since last run: warn user and\n   316→                     force re-run of the extract step regardless of gate state.\n   317→                     (See §7.3 for stale-spec detection.)\n   318→\n   319→  --dry-run          Print step plan and gate criteria to stdout. Exit without\n   320→                     launching any subprocesses.\n   321→\n   322→  --model TEXT       Override model for all steps. Normally model is set\n   323→                     per-agent for generate steps; this flag overrides all.\n   324→\n   325→  --max-turns INT    Max turns passed to each claude -p invocation.\n   326→                     Default: 50\n   327→\n   328→  --debug            Enable debug logging to output_dir/roadmap-debug.log\n   329→```\n   330→\n   331→### Registration in `main.py`\n   332→\n   333→```python\n   334→from superclaude.cli.roadmap import roadmap_group\n   335→main.add_command(roadmap_group, name=\"roadmap\")\n   336→```\n   337→\n   338→---\n   339→\n   340→## 6. Failure Policy\n   341→\n   342→### 6.1 Step Execution Flow\n   343→\n   344→```\n   345→for each step (in order):\n   346→  attempt 1:\n   347→    launch claude -p subprocess\n   348→    wait for subprocess exit (with timeout)\n   349→    run gate_passed()\n   350→    if gate passes → record StepResult(PASS, attempt=1), continue to next step\n   351→    if gate fails  → log gate_failure_reason, proceed to attempt 2\n   352→    if timeout     → log timeout, proceed to attempt 2\n   353→\n   354→  attempt 2 (retry):\n   355→    same prompt, same inputs, fresh subprocess\n   356→    run gate_passed()\n   357→    if gate passes → record StepResult(PASS, attempt=2), continue to next step\n   358→    if gate fails  → HALT: record StepResult(FAIL), report to user, exit non-zero\n   359→    if timeout     → HALT: record StepResult(TIMEOUT), report to user, exit non-zero\n   360→```\n   361→\n   362→Parallel steps (generate-A, generate-B): each follows this flow independently. If either halts, the pipeline halts — the other subprocess is terminated.\n   363→\n   364→### 6.2 HALT Output\n   365→\n   366→On halt, the CLI prints to stderr:\n   367→\n   368→```\n   369→ERROR: Roadmap pipeline halted at step 'generate-opus-architect' (attempt 2/2)\n   370→  Gate failure: Missing required frontmatter field 'primary_persona' in roadmap-opus-architect.md\n   371→  Output file: .dev/releases/current/v2.07/roadmap-opus-architect.md\n   372→  Output size: 847 bytes (86 lines)\n   373→  Step timeout: 900s | Elapsed: 234s\n   374→\n   375→Completed steps: extract (PASS, attempt 1)\n   376→Failed step:     generate-opus-architect (FAIL, attempt 2)\n   377→Skipped steps:   generate-haiku-architect, diff, debate, score, merge, test-strategy\n   378→\n   379→To retry from this step:\n   380→  superclaude roadmap spec.md --resume\n   381→\n   382→To inspect the failing output:\n   383→  cat .dev/releases/current/v2.07/roadmap-opus-architect.md\n   384→```\n   385→\n   386→### 6.3 Resume Behavior\n   387→\n   388→`--resume` checks each step's gate in order. The first step that fails its gate is re-run (with its full 2-attempt retry policy). All prior steps that pass their gates are skipped.\n   389→\n   390→**Stale spec detection**: On `--resume`, the CLI computes a SHA-256 hash of the spec-file and compares it to a hash stored in `output_dir/.roadmap-state.json` (written after the extract step passes). If the hashes differ:\n   391→\n   392→```\n   393→WARNING: spec-file has changed since last run.\n   394→  Last run: 2026-03-04T18:22:00Z  hash: abc123...\n   395→  Current:                         hash: def456...\n   396→\n   397→The extraction artifact may be stale. Forcing re-run of extract step.\n   398→Other completed steps will be reused if their gates still pass.\n   399→\n   400→Continue? [Y/n]\n   401→```\n   402→\n   403→The extract step is always re-run when the spec hash changes, regardless of whether `extraction.md` passes its gate.\n   404→\n   405→---\n   406→\n   407→## 7. Progress Display\n   408→\n   409→While a step is running, the CLI emits to stdout:\n   410→\n   411→```\n   412→[roadmap] Step 2/7: generate-opus-architect\n   413→  Model:   claude opus (architect)\n   414→  Timeout: 900s\n   415→  Elapsed: 00:01:43 ...\n   416→```\n   417→\n   418→Updated every 5 seconds (overwrite the same line using `\\r`). The executor builds the prompt by calling the step's prompt builder function (in `roadmap/prompts.py`) with the paths of the step's `inputs` list. No shared in-memory state passes between steps. Each subprocess is a fresh `claude -p` invocation with no session continuity.\n\nPrompt injection pattern (enforced by executor):\n```\nclaude -p \"<step.prompt>\" \\\n  --file <input_1> \\\n  --file <input_2> \\\n  --model <agent.model> \\\n  --max-turns <config.max_turns> \\\n  <config.permission_flag>\n```\n\nThe executor does not pass `--continue` or any session ID between steps.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Pipeline Steps\n\nSteps 2a and 2b (generate-A and generate-B) run as concurrent subprocesses. Step 3a (diff) waits for both generate steps' gates to pass before starting.\n\nAll other steps are sequential.\n\n### Step Definitions\n\n| ID | Name | Inputs | Output file | Required frontmatter fields | Min lines | Timeout |\n|----|------|--------|-------------|----------------------------|-----------|---------|\n| `extract` | Extract requirements | spec-file | `extraction.md` | `functional_requirements`, `complexity_score`, `complexity_class` | 50 | 300s |\n| `generate-{agent.id}` | Generate variant (×2, parallel) | extraction.md | `roadmap-{agent.id}.md` | `spec_source`, `complexity_score`, `primary_persona` | 100 | 900s |\n| `diff` | Diff analysis | roadmap-A.md, roadmap-B.md | `diff-analysis.md` | `total_diff_points`, `shared_assumptions_count` | 30 | 300s |\n| `debate` | Structured debate | diff-analysis.md, roadmap-A.md, roadmap-B.md | `debate-transcript.md` | `convergence_score`, `rounds_completed` | 50 | 600s |\n| `score` | Base selection + scoring | debate-transcript.md, roadmap-A.md, roadmap-B.md | `base-selection.md` | `base_variant`, `variant_scores` | 20 | 300s |\n| `merge` | Merge to final roadmap | base-selection.md, roadmap-A.md, roadmap-B.md, debate-transcript.md | `roadmap.md` | `spec_source`, `complexity_score`, `adversarial` | 150 | 600s |\n| `test-strategy` | Test strategy | roadmap.md, extraction.md | `test-strategy.md` | `validation_milestones`, `interleave_ratio` | 40 | 300s |\n\n**Timeout rationale**:\n- `generate-{agent}`: 900s (15 min) — full roadmap generation with adversarial variant is the most expensive single step\n- `debate`: 600s (10 min) — structured multi-round debate\n- `merge`: 600s (10 min) — synthesis across multiple large artifacts\n- All other steps: 300s (5 min) — bounded, single-concern tasks\n\n**Semantic checks for STRICT-tier steps** (v1):\n<!-- Source: Variant B, Strategy 5 — merged per Change #5 -->\n\nThe `merge` step includes these additional `SemanticCheck` instances:\n- `no_heading_gaps`: No heading level gaps (e.g., H2 → H4 without H3)\n- `cross_refs_resolve`: All \"See §X\" and \"Section X.Y\" references resolve to existing headings\n- `no_duplicate_headings`: No duplicate H2 or H3 heading text\n\nThe `generate-{agent}` steps include:\n- `frontmatter_values_non_empty`: All required frontmatter fields have non-empty values\n- `has_actionable_content`: At least one section contains numbered or bulleted items (not prose-only)\n\nThe `debate` step includes:\n- `convergence_score_valid`: `convergence_score` frontmatter value parses as float in [0.0, 1.0]\n\n### Step Output Directory\n\nAll output files are written to `config.output_dir`. By default this is the parent directory of `spec_file`:\n\n```\nspec:   .dev/releases/current/v2.07/spec.md\noutput: .dev/releases/current/v2.07/\n  extraction.md\n  roadmap-opus-architect.md\n  roadmap-haiku-architect.md\n  diff-analysis.md\n  debate-transcript.md\n  base-selection.md\n  roadmap.md\n  test-strategy.md\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. CLI Interface\n\n```\nsuperclaude roadmap <spec-file> [OPTIONS]\n\nArguments:\n  spec-file          Path to specification markdown file (required)\n\nOptions:\n  --agents TEXT      Comma-separated agent specs: model[:persona]\n                     Default: \"opus:architect,haiku:architect\"\n                     Model shorthand (opus/sonnet/haiku) passed directly to\n                     claude CLI — no resolution required.\n\n  --output PATH      Output directory for all artifacts.\n                     Default: parent directory of spec-file.\n\n  --depth [quick|standard|deep]\n                     Controls debate step round count.\n                     quick=1 round, standard=2, deep=3.\n                     Default: standard\n\n  --resume           Skip steps whose output files already pass their gates.\n                     Re-run from the first step that fails its gate.\n                     If spec-file has changed since last run: warn user and\n                     force re-run of the extract step regardless of gate state.\n                     (See §7.3 for stale-spec detection.)\n\n  --dry-run          Print step plan and gate criteria to stdout. Exit without\n                     launching any subprocesses.\n\n  --model TEXT       Override model for all steps. Normally model is set\n                     per-agent for generate steps; this flag overrides all.\n\n  --max-turns INT    Max turns passed to each claude -p invocation.\n                     Default: 50\n\n  --debug            Enable debug logging to output_dir/roadmap-debug.log\n```\n\n### Registration in `main.py`\n\n```python\nfrom superclaude.cli.roadmap import roadmap_group\nmain.add_command(roadmap_group, name=\"roadmap\")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Failure Policy\n\n### 6.1 Step Execution Flow\n\n```\nfor each step (in order):\n  attempt 1:\n    launch claude -p subprocess\n    wait for subprocess exit (with timeout)\n    run gate_passed()\n    if gate passes → record StepResult(PASS, attempt=1), continue to next step\n    if gate fails  → log gate_failure_reason, proceed to attempt 2\n    if timeout     → log timeout, proceed to attempt 2\n\n  attempt 2 (retry):\n    same prompt, same inputs, fresh subprocess\n    run gate_passed()\n    if gate passes → record StepResult(PASS, attempt=2), continue to next step\n    if gate fails  → HALT: record StepResult(FAIL), report to user, exit non-zero\n    if timeout     → HALT: record StepResult(TIMEOUT), report to user, exit non-zero\n```\n\nParallel steps (generate-A, generate-B): each follows this flow independently. If either halts, the pipeline halts — the other subprocess is terminated.\n\n### 6.2 HALT Output\n\nOn halt, the CLI prints to stderr:\n\n```\nERROR: Roadmap pipeline halted at step 'generate-opus-architect' (attempt 2/2)\n  Gate failure: Missing required frontmatter field 'primary_persona' in roadmap-opus-architect.md\n  Output file: .dev/releases/current/v2.07/roadmap-opus-architect.md\n  Output size: 847 bytes (86 lines)\n  Step timeout: 900s | Elapsed: 234s\n\nCompleted steps: extract (PASS, attempt 1)\nFailed step:     generate-opus-architect (FAIL, attempt 2)\nSkipped steps:   generate-haiku-architect, diff, debate, score, merge, test-strategy\n\nTo retry from this step:\n  superclaude roadmap spec.md --resume\n\nTo inspect the failing output:\n  cat .dev/releases/current/v2.07/roadmap-opus-architect.md\n```\n\n### 6.3 Resume Behavior\n\n`--resume` checks each step's gate in order. The first step that fails its gate is re-run (with its full 2-attempt retry policy). All prior steps that pass their gates are skipped.\n\n**Stale spec detection**: On `--resume`, the CLI computes a SHA-256 hash of the spec-file and compares it to a hash stored in `output_dir/.roadmap-state.json` (written after the extract step passes). If the hashes differ:\n\n```\nWARNING: spec-file has changed since last run.\n  Last run: 2026-03-04T18:22:00Z  hash: abc123...\n  Current:                         hash: def456...\n\nThe extraction artifact may be stale. Forcing re-run of extract step.\nOther completed steps will be reused if their gates still pass.\n\nContinue? [Y/n]\n```\n\nThe extract step is always re-run when the spec hash changes, regardless of whether `extraction.md` passes its gate.\n\n---\n\n## 7. Progress Display\n\nWhile a step is running, the CLI emits to stdout:\n\n```\n[roadmap] Step 2/7: generate-opus-architect\n  Model:   claude opus (architect)\n  Timeout: 900s\n  Elapsed: 00:01:43 ...\n```\n\nUpdated every 5 seconds (overwrite the same line using `\\r`). On step completion:\n\n```\n[roadmap] Step 2/7: generate-opus-architect  PASS (attempt 1, 1m43s)\n           Gate: roadmap-opus-architect.md — 312 lines, frontmatter OK\n```\n\nOn parallel steps:\n\n```\n[roadmap] Step 2a/7: generate-opus-architect   00:01:43 ...\n[roadmap] Step 2b/7: generate-haiku-architect  00:01:21 ...\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Functional Requirements\n\n| ID | Requirement | Source |\n|----|-------------|--------|\n| FR-01 | `superclaude roadmap <spec>` executes steps in the defined sequence with gates enforced between each step | Core |\n| FR-02 | Steps generate-A and generate-B launch as concurrent subprocesses; step diff waits for both gates to pass | Core |\n| FR-03 | Each step's prompt is built from only the files in its `inputs` list; no other context is passed to the subprocess | Core |\n| FR-04 | `gate_passed()` checks: file exists AND non-empty AND line count >= minimum AND YAML frontmatter parseable AND all required fields present | Wiegers |\n| FR-05 | On gate failure: retry once (same prompt), then halt with diagnostic output per §6.2 | Core |\n| FR-06 | `--resume` skips steps whose output files pass their gates; forces extract re-run if spec-file hash changed | Newman |\n| FR-07 | `--dry-run` prints step plan (step ID, output file, gate criteria, timeout) and exits without subprocess invocations | Core |\n| FR-08 | Default output directory is the parent directory of the spec-file | Core |\n| FR-09 | `superclaude roadmap` registered as a Click command group in `main.py` | Core |\n| FR-10 | Sprint module migrated to import `ClaudeProcess`, generic step execution from `pipeline/`; sprint's external CLI API unchanged | Fowler |\n| FR-11 | `gate_passed()` returns `(bool, str | None)` — failure reason is a human-readable string per the defined message format | Adzic |\n| FR-12 | `.roadmap-state.json` written to `output_dir` after extract step passes, containing spec-file SHA-256 hash and timestamp | Newman |\n| FR-13 | Progress output emitted to stdout during step execution per §7 | Nygard |\n| FR-14 | Per-step timeouts enforced per the timeout values in §4 | Nygard |\n| FR-15 | `--agents` value is passed directly to `claude -p --model`; no model ID resolution performed by the CLI | Core |\n\n---\n\n## 9. Acceptance Criteria\n\nEnd-to-end acceptance tests (not unit tests — these validate the full CLI):\n\n**AC-01**: Given a valid spec-file, `superclaude roadmap spec.md --dry-run` prints 7 step entries (each with ID, output filename, gate criteria, timeout) and exits 0. No files written.\n\n**AC-02**: Given a valid spec-file, `superclaude roadmap spec.md` completes all 7 steps and writes 8 files to output-dir: `extraction.md`, `roadmap-opus-architect.md`, `roadmap-haiku-architect.md`, `diff-analysis.md`, `debate-transcript.md`, `base-selection.md`, `roadmap.md`, `test-strategy.md`.\n\n**AC-03**: Given a generate step that produces a file missing the `primary_persona` frontmatter field, the CLI retries once, then halts and prints the gate failure message containing the field name and file path. Exits non-zero.\n\n**AC-04**: Given a completed run (all gates pass), `superclaude roadmap spec.md --resume` prints `Skipping N steps (gates pass)` and exits 0 without launching any subprocesses.\n\n**AC-05**: Given a completed run followed by a spec-file modification, `superclaude roadmap spec.md --resume` detects the hash mismatch, prints the stale-spec warning, and re-runs the extract step.\n\n**AC-06**: `uv run pytest tests/sprint/` exits 0 after the pipeline/ migration (sprint external API unchanged).\n\n**AC-07**: `superclaude roadmap spec.md --agents sonnet:security,haiku:qa` uses `sonnet` and `haiku` as the model values in the two generate step subprocess invocations (verified via `--dry-run` output showing model per step).\n\n---\n\n## 11. Open Questions & Deferred Features\n\n| Question | Resolution |\n|----------|-----------|\n| Debate step granularity | 3 gated sub-steps: diff → debate → score (then merge as step 4) |\n| PR strategy | Single PR: pipeline/ extraction + sprint migration + roadmap/ |\n| Model shorthand resolution | Not needed — claude CLI accepts opus/sonnet/haiku natively |\n\n### Deferred Features (v1.1+)\n<!-- Source: Variant B (tasklist-strategies), v1.1 deferral table — merged per Change #6 -->","numLines":300,"startLine":200,"totalLines":1097}}}
